<s> he took it with some natural suspicion and approached it to his nose <\s>

<s> slightly reassured he raised his eyes to the young man's face <\s>
<s> it had rather fawn like ears a laughing mouth with half a toothbrush growing out of it on each side and small lively eyes above a normally dressed appearance <\s>
<s> thank you he said and moved by a sort of irritation added glad to hear you like beauty that's rare nowadays <\s>
<s> i dote on it said the young man but you and i are the last of the old guard sir <\s>

<s> i'll drop in like a bird <\s>
<s> and he took off his hat <\s>
<s> soames already regretting his impulse raised his own slightly in response with a downward look at the young man's companion who had a purple tie dreadful little sluglike whiskers and a scornful look as if he were a poet <\s>
<s> it was the first indiscretion he had committed for so long that he went and sat down in an alcove <\s>
<s> what had possessed him to give his card to a rackety young fellow who went about with a thing like that <\s>
<s> and fleur always at the back of his thoughts started out like a filigree figure from a clock when the hour strikes <\s>

<s> why even since the post impressionists there had been one or two painters not to be sneezed at <\s>
<s> during the thirty eight years of his connoisseur's life indeed he had marked so many movements seen the tides of taste and technique so ebb and flow that there was really no telling anything except that there was money to be made out of every change of fashion <\s>
<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>
<s> he got up and stood before the picture trying hard to see it with the eyes of other people <\s>
<s> above the tomato blobs was what he took to be a sunset till some one passing said he's got the airplanes wonderfully don't you think <\s>
<s> below the tomato blobs was a band of white with vertical black stripes to which he could assign no meaning whatever till some one else came by murmuring what expression he gets with his foreground <\s>
<s> soames went back to his seat <\s>
<s> the thing was rich as his father would have said and he wouldn't give a damn for it <\s>
<s> they were all expressionists now he had heard on the continent <\s>
<s> so it was coming here too was it <\s>

<s> he wondered where this this expressionism had been hatched <\s>
<s> the thing was a regular disease <\s>
<s> he had become conscious of a woman and a youth standing between him and the future town <\s>

<s> no mistaking that back elegant as ever though the hair above had gone grey <\s>

<s> grudgingly he admitted her still beautiful and in figure almost as young as ever <\s>

<s> if she saw him all the better <\s>

<s> then half conscious that such a thought was extravagant for a forsyte of his age soames took out his watch <\s>

<s> murmured soames the turf's in danger <\s>

<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>

<s> that was the negation of all virtue the overturning of all forsyte principles <\s>
<s> could civilization be built on any other <\s>
<s> he did not think so <\s>
<s> well they wouldn't confiscate his pictures for they wouldn't know their worth <\s>
<s> but what would they be worth if these maniacs once began to milk capital <\s>
<s> a drug on the market <\s>
<s> i don't care about myself he thought i could live on five hundred a year and never know the difference at my age <\s>
<s> this fortune so widely invested these treasures so carefully chosen and amassed were all for her <\s>
<s> and if it should turn out that he couldn't give or leave them to her well life had no meaning and what was the use of going in to look at this crazy futuristic stuff with the view of seeing whether it had any future <\s>
<s> arriving at the gallery off cork street however he paid his shilling picked up a catalogue and entered <\s>
<s> some ten persons were prowling round <\s>
<s> soames took steps and came on what looked to him like a lamp post bent by collision with a motor omnibus <\s>
<s> it was advanced some three paces from the wall and was described in his catalogue as jupiter <\s>
<s> he examined it with curiosity having recently turned some of his attention to sculpture <\s>
<s> if that's jupiter he thought i wonder what juno's like <\s>
<s> and suddenly he saw her opposite <\s>
<s> she appeared to him like nothing so much as a pump with two handles lightly clad in snow <\s>
<s> he was still gazing at her when two of the prowlers halted on his left <\s>
<s> he heard one say <\s>
<s> growled soames to himself <\s>
<s> the other's boyish voice replied missed it old bean he's pulling your leg <\s>
<s> when jove and juno created he them he was saying i'll see how much these fools will swallow <\s>
<s> and they've lapped up the lot <\s>
<s> vospovitch is an innovator <\s>
<s> don't you see that he's brought satire into sculpture <\s>
<s> the future of plastic art of music painting and even architecture has set in satiric <\s>
<s> it was bound to <\s>
<s> people are tired the bottom's tumbled out of sentiment <\s>
<s> well i'm quite equal to taking a little interest in beauty <\s>
<s> i was through the war <\s>
<s> you've dropped your handkerchief sir <\s>
<s> soames saw a handkerchief held out in front of him <\s>
<s> he took it with some natural suspicion and approached it to his nose <\s>
<s> it had the right scent of distant eau de cologne and his initials in a corner <\s>
<s> slightly reassured he raised his eyes to the young man's face <\s>
<s> it had rather fawn like ears a laughing mouth with half a toothbrush growing out of it on each side and small lively eyes above a normally dressed appearance <\s>
<s> thank you he said and moved by a sort of irritation added glad to hear you like beauty that's rare nowadays <\s>
<s> i dote on it said the young man but you and i are the last of the old guard sir <\s>
<s> if you really care for pictures he said here's my card <\s>
<s> i can show you some quite good ones any sunday if you're down the river and care to look in <\s>
<s> awfully nice of you sir <\s>
<s> i'll drop in like a bird <\s>
<s> and he took off his hat <\s>
<s> soames already regretting his impulse raised his own slightly in response with a downward look at the young man's companion who had a purple tie dreadful little sluglike whiskers and a scornful look as if he were a poet <\s>
<s> it was the first indiscretion he had committed for so long that he went and sat down in an alcove <\s>
<s> what had possessed him to give his card to a rackety young fellow who went about with a thing like that <\s>
<s> and fleur always at the back of his thoughts started out like a filigree figure from a clock when the hour strikes <\s>
<s> on the screen opposite the alcove was a large canvas with a great many square tomato coloured blobs on it and nothing else so far as soames could see from where he sat <\s>
<s> he looked at his catalogue no <\s>
<s> 32 the future town' paul post <\s>
<s> i suppose that's satiric too he thought <\s>
<s> but his second impulse was more cautious <\s>
<s> it did not do to condemn hurriedly <\s>
<s> there had been those stripey streaky creations of monet's which had turned out such trumps and then the stippled school and gauguin <\s>
<s> why even since the post impressionists there had been one or two painters not to be sneezed at <\s>
<s> during the thirty eight years of his connoisseur's life indeed he had marked so many movements seen the tides of taste and technique so ebb and flow that there was really no telling anything except that there was money to be made out of every change of fashion <\s>
<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>
<s> he got up and stood before the picture trying hard to see it with the eyes of other people <\s>
<s> above the tomato blobs was what he took to be a sunset till some one passing said he's got the airplanes wonderfully don't you think <\s>
<s> below the tomato blobs was a band of white with vertical black stripes to which he could assign no meaning whatever till some one else came by murmuring what expression he gets with his foreground <\s>
<s> soames went back to his seat <\s>
<s> the thing was rich as his father would have said and he wouldn't give a damn for it <\s>
<s> they were all expressionists now he had heard on the continent <\s>
<s> so it was coming here too was it <\s>
<s> he remembered the first wave of influenza in 1887 or 8 hatched in china so they said <\s>
<s> he wondered where this this expressionism had been hatched <\s>
<s> the thing was a regular disease <\s>
<s> he had become conscious of a woman and a youth standing between him and the future town <\s>
<s> their backs were turned but very suddenly soames put his catalogue before his face and drawing his hat forward gazed through the slit between <\s>
<s> no mistaking that back elegant as ever though the hair above had gone grey <\s>
<s> and this no doubt was her son by that fellow jolyon forsyte their boy six months older than his own girl <\s>
<s> and mumbling over in his mind the bitter days of his divorce he rose to get out of sight but quickly sat down again <\s>
<s> she had turned her head to speak to her boy her profile was still so youthful that it made her grey hair seem powdery as if fancy dressed and her lips were smiling as soames first possessor of them had never seen them smile <\s>
<s> grudgingly he admitted her still beautiful and in figure almost as young as ever <\s>
<s> and how that boy smiled back at her <\s>
<s> emotion squeezed soames heart <\s>
<s> the sight infringed his sense of justice <\s>
<s> he grudged her that boy's smile it went beyond what fleur gave him and it was undeserved <\s>
<s> their son might have been his son fleur might have been her daughter if she had kept straight <\s>
<s> he lowered his catalogue <\s>
<s> if she saw him all the better <\s>
<s> a reminder of her conduct in the presence of her son who probably knew nothing of it would be a salutary touch from the finger of that nemesis which surely must soon or late visit her <\s>
<s> then half conscious that such a thought was extravagant for a forsyte of his age soames took out his watch <\s>
<s> she had gone to his niece imogen cardigan's and there they would keep her smoking cigarettes and gossiping and that <\s>
<s> he heard the boy laugh and say eagerly i say mum is this by one of auntie june's lame ducks <\s>
<s> paul post i believe it is darling <\s>
<s> the word produced a little shock in soames he had never heard her use it <\s>
<s> and then she saw him <\s>
<s> his eyes must have had in them something of george forsyte's sardonic look for her gloved hand crisped the folds of her frock her eyebrows rose her face went stony <\s>
<s> it is a caution said the boy catching her arm again <\s>
<s> murmured soames the turf's in danger <\s>
<s> over george's face moved a gleam of sardonic self defence <\s>
<s> well he said they brought me up to do nothing and here i am in the sear and yellow getting poorer every day <\s>
<s> these labour chaps mean to have the lot before they've done <\s>
<s> what are you going to do for a living when it comes <\s>
<s> i shall work a six hour day teaching politicians how to see a joke <\s>
<s> take my tip soames go into parliament make sure of your four hundred and employ me <\s>
<s> and as soames retired he resumed his seat in the bay window <\s>

<s> he examined it with curiosity having recently turned some of his attention to sculpture <\s>
<s> if that's jupiter he thought i wonder what juno's like <\s>
<s> and suddenly he saw her opposite <\s>
<s> she appeared to him like nothing so much as a pump with two handles lightly clad in snow <\s>
<s> he was still gazing at her when two of the prowlers halted on his left <\s>
<s> he heard one say <\s>
<s> growled soames to himself <\s>

<s> i was through the war <\s>
<s> you've dropped your handkerchief sir <\s>
<s> soames saw a handkerchief held out in front of him <\s>
<s> he took it with some natural suspicion and approached it to his nose <\s>
<s> it had the right scent of distant eau de cologne and his initials in a corner <\s>
<s> slightly reassured he raised his eyes to the young man's face <\s>
<s> it had rather fawn like ears a laughing mouth with half a toothbrush growing out of it on each side and small lively eyes above a normally dressed appearance <\s>
<s> thank you he said and moved by a sort of irritation added glad to hear you like beauty that's rare nowadays <\s>
<s> i dote on it said the young man but you and i are the last of the old guard sir <\s>
<s> if you really care for pictures he said here's my card <\s>
<s> i can show you some quite good ones any sunday if you're down the river and care to look in <\s>

<s> i'll drop in like a bird <\s>
<s> and he took off his hat <\s>
<s> soames already regretting his impulse raised his own slightly in response with a downward look at the young man's companion who had a purple tie dreadful little sluglike whiskers and a scornful look as if he were a poet <\s>
<s> it was the first indiscretion he had committed for so long that he went and sat down in an alcove <\s>
<s> what had possessed him to give his card to a rackety young fellow who went about with a thing like that <\s>
<s> and fleur always at the back of his thoughts started out like a filigree figure from a clock when the hour strikes <\s>

<s> he looked at his catalogue no <\s>
<s> 32 the future town' paul post <\s>
<s> i suppose that's satiric too he thought <\s>
<s> but his second impulse was more cautious <\s>
<s> it did not do to condemn hurriedly <\s>
<s> there had been those stripey streaky creations of monet's which had turned out such trumps and then the stippled school and gauguin <\s>
<s> why even since the post impressionists there had been one or two painters not to be sneezed at <\s>
<s> during the thirty eight years of his connoisseur's life indeed he had marked so many movements seen the tides of taste and technique so ebb and flow that there was really no telling anything except that there was money to be made out of every change of fashion <\s>
<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>
<s> he got up and stood before the picture trying hard to see it with the eyes of other people <\s>
<s> above the tomato blobs was what he took to be a sunset till some one passing said he's got the airplanes wonderfully don't you think <\s>
<s> below the tomato blobs was a band of white with vertical black stripes to which he could assign no meaning whatever till some one else came by murmuring what expression he gets with his foreground <\s>
<s> soames went back to his seat <\s>
<s> the thing was rich as his father would have said and he wouldn't give a damn for it <\s>
<s> they were all expressionists now he had heard on the continent <\s>
<s> so it was coming here too was it <\s>

<s> he wondered where this this expressionism had been hatched <\s>
<s> the thing was a regular disease <\s>
<s> he had become conscious of a woman and a youth standing between him and the future town <\s>
<s> their backs were turned but very suddenly soames put his catalogue before his face and drawing his hat forward gazed through the slit between <\s>
<s> no mistaking that back elegant as ever though the hair above had gone grey <\s>
<s> and this no doubt was her son by that fellow jolyon forsyte their boy six months older than his own girl <\s>
<s> and mumbling over in his mind the bitter days of his divorce he rose to get out of sight but quickly sat down again <\s>
<s> she had turned her head to speak to her boy her profile was still so youthful that it made her grey hair seem powdery as if fancy dressed and her lips were smiling as soames first possessor of them had never seen them smile <\s>
<s> grudgingly he admitted her still beautiful and in figure almost as young as ever <\s>
<s> and how that boy smiled back at her <\s>

<s> the sight infringed his sense of justice <\s>

<s> he lowered his catalogue <\s>
<s> if she saw him all the better <\s>
<s> a reminder of her conduct in the presence of her son who probably knew nothing of it would be a salutary touch from the finger of that nemesis which surely must soon or late visit her <\s>
<s> then half conscious that such a thought was extravagant for a forsyte of his age soames took out his watch <\s>
<s> she had gone to his niece imogen cardigan's and there they would keep her smoking cigarettes and gossiping and that <\s>

<s> the word produced a little shock in soames he had never heard her use it <\s>
<s> and then she saw him <\s>

<s> murmured soames the turf's in danger <\s>
<s> over george's face moved a gleam of sardonic self defence <\s>
<s> well he said they brought me up to do nothing and here i am in the sear and yellow getting poorer every day <\s>
<s> these labour chaps mean to have the lot before they've done <\s>
<s> what are you going to do for a living when it comes <\s>
<s> i shall work a six hour day teaching politicians how to see a joke <\s>
<s> take my tip soames go into parliament make sure of your four hundred and employ me <\s>
<s> and as soames retired he resumed his seat in the bay window <\s>

<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>

<s> this too might quite well be a case where one must subdue primordial instinct or lose the market <\s>

<s> he examined it with curiosity having recently turned some of his attention to sculpture <\s>
<s> if that's jupiter he thought i wonder what juno's like <\s>
<s> and suddenly he saw her opposite <\s>

<s> soames saw a handkerchief held out in front of him <\s>
<s> he took it with some natural suspicion and approached it to his nose <\s>

<s> slightly reassured he raised his eyes to the young man's face <\s>
<s> it had rather fawn like ears a laughing mouth with half a toothbrush growing out of it on each side and small lively eyes above a normally dressed appearance <\s>
<s> thank you he said and moved by a sort of irritation added glad to hear you like beauty that's rare nowadays <\s>
<s> i dote on it said the young man but you and i are the last of the old guard sir <\s>

<s> i'll drop in like a bird <\s>
<s> and he took off his hat <\s>
<s> soames already regretting his impulse raised his own slightly in response with a downward look at the young man's companion who had a purple tie dreadful little sluglike whiskers and a scornful look as if he were a poet <\s>
<s> it was the first indiscretion he had committed for so long that he went and sat down in an alcove <\s>

<s> i suppose that's satiric too he thought <\s>

<s> he got up and stood before the picture trying hard to see it with the eyes of other people <\s>

<s> the thing was rich as his father would have said and he wouldn't give a damn for it <\s>

<s> if she saw him all the better <\s>
